This fix should be applied AFTER the material is fetched from database (around line 5502). FORMULA VERIFICATION: The GSM-based formula implementation is correct: 1) linear_metres_per_tonne = 1,000,000 / (GSM Ã— width_metres), 2) cost_per_meter = price_per_tonne / linear_metres_per_tonne, 3) material_cost = strip_length_m Ã— cost_per_meter Ã— projected_qty.
